Thank you to all the shuttle bus drivers for taking us to the various facilities of the resort in the sub-zero cold. Especially the driver Xiao Luo; he took us to have breakfast every morning. Hantian Resort has completely changed from seven years ago. It has become a complete integrated eating, drinking, playing and parent-child park. There are too many high-quality experiences that can be described after this experience. It is impossible to list them one by one. Hantian's service is very good from the lobby, guest rooms, and catering. Only the level of some service staff in the hot spring needs to be improved. Dinner was still in the Chinese restaurant. The taste was as good as ever. The chopped pepper fish head that I waited for 40 minutes was delicious. Now Hantian's spicy dishes have also improved. The level of waiters is getting higher and higher. From the waiter sister to the supervisor, they are very proactive in service. Thumbs up. The gifts from Hantian this time were all great, whether it was snacks or fruits, including the sweet soup in the evening, which was great, and the turndown service was really a five-star standard. However, the entertainment and hot spring facilities in the resort have to be paid separately and are not included in the high room rate. msg:During the Dragon Boat Festival holiday, I took my family to Yangxin Valley for vacation. The Qinglianju two-bedroom and one-living room hotel I stayed in was suitable for a family. The room was clean and sanitary, and there were fruit snacks and goodnight desserts every day. They were available at any time for any needs. The environment was also very good, the breakfast tasted good, and there was no need to go to the main building to squeeze in. The whole resort was very large, and there were many places for children to play, such as go-karts, bed-bumping, horseback riding, and two outdoor parks, one Jurassic Park and one Shanhaijing Park. There were also many places to eat, including a Chinese restaurant, a Hong Kong-style tea restaurant, Japanese cuisine, a fish pier, and an earth stove. They were not repeated for several days, and the taste and price were all good. It felt very good to rest in the room and look at the scenery on the last afternoon. A family should relax and rest when on vacation. Special thanks to the service staff of the park, from the butler to the shuttle bus pick-up master, from the front desk to the restaurant service staff, as well as the administrator of the Shanhaijing Park and the waiters at the mountaintop observation deck. They were all very friendly and had a strong sense of service. It felt like family. When they left, they also gave them a lot of snacks, fruit snacks and vegetables they grew themselves, which the children especially loved. I look forward to coming again next time!
